[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Remote working experience with 10 questions:

**How often do you work remotely?**
  - Daily
  - Several times a week
  - Occasionally
  - Rarely
  - Never

**What do you think are the most significant benefits of remote working for you? (Select all that apply)**
  - Increased flexibility and work-life balance
  - Reduced commuting time and expenses
  - Improved productivity and focus
  - Enhanced job satisfaction and autonomy
  - Other (please specify)

**Have you experienced any challenges or difficulties while working remotely? If so, please describe.**

**How do you stay connected and communicate with your team and colleagues while working remotely?**
  - Email
  - Instant messaging apps (e.g. Slack, Microsoft Teams)
  - Video conferencing tools (e.g. Zoom, Google Meet)
  - Phone calls
  - In-person meetings (when possible)
  - Other (please specify)

**Do you feel that remote working has improved your overall job satisfaction and well-being?**
  - Yes
  - No
  - Neutral

**What tools or software do you use to stay organized and manage your work while working remotely? (Select all that apply)**
  - Task management tools (e.g. Trello, Asana)
  - Project management software (e.g. Basecamp, Jira)
  - Time tracking software (e.g. Harvest, Toggl)
  - Note-taking apps (e.g. Evernote, OneNote)
  - Other (please specify)

**How do you prioritize your tasks and manage your time while working remotely?**
  - Create a daily schedule
  - Use a task list or to-do list
  - Focus on most important tasks first
  - Take regular breaks
  - Other (please specify)

**Do you feel that remote working has impacted your work-life balance? If so, how?**
  - Positively (more time for personal activities)
  - Negatively (difficulty disconnecting from work)
  - No impact
  - Other (please specify)

**How do you handle distractions or interruptions while working remotely?**
  - Create a dedicated workspace
  - Use noise-cancelling headphones or music
  - Set boundaries with family or roommates
  - Take regular breaks
  - Other (please specify)

**Do you feel that remote working has affected your physical and mental health? If so, how?**
  - Positively (less stress, more exercise)
  - Negatively (more sedentary, increased stress)
  - No impact
  - Other (please specify)

**Any additional comments or suggestions regarding remote working experience?**
